It is almost certain that they are descended from the European family of Jass games, which originated in the Netherlands. There are eight cards in each of the usual French suits: Hearts, Diamonds, Clubs and spades. In 29 card game the cards in every suit rank from high to low: J-9-A-10-K-Q-8-7.\r\n\r\nThe player need to bid and set a target for themselves and then achieve it. The player who wins the bid get to set the trump suit. Play is typically counter-clockwise; the player to the right of the dealer plays to the first trick.
